The extension pauses all sort of window opening requests for user attention. You can either accept or deny a request. Multiple unique requests are shown in an array. If a websites requests a single URL more than once, a badge number will be shown indicating the total number of requests to this particular URL.\r\n\r\n\r\nPlease note that the extension is recently renamed from \"Popup Blocker (ultimate)\" to \"Popup Blocker (strict)\"\r\n\r\nOptions:\r\n1.
